 pehla, kashmir mudde kaa samaadhaan talashna
 Both governments appear to be in a mood to deny the achievements that led to the issuance of the Islamabad manifesto during Atal Bihari Vajpayee's visit to Islamabad in January 2004, and negotiations between Satinder Lamba and Tariq Aziz in the same year under back-door policy Achieved in the following three years
 dastavej bataate hai ki vaartakaron ne is baat par sahmati jataai thi ki jammu-kashmir ke masale ke antim hal main seemaa or aam logon kii adla-badali se parhez rakhana hoga, or hamen line of control ke aar-paar mitron or sambandhiyon kii awajahi badhaane par dhyaan dena hoga

 yah sahi he ki back-door policy ke tahat hasil kii gai is sahmati ko donon main se kisi bhi sarkaar ke samaksh pushti ke liye nahin laayaa gaya, lekin chunki vaartakar apni-apni sarkaron ke pratinidhi ke taur par baat kar rahe the, aise main yah to kaha hi ja saktaa he ki baatcheet se sarkaar ke prastaavon ke bare main kuch andaja to lagata hi he

 They get hit
 unki sampatti kaa bhi nuksaan hota he, or kai baar unhen visthapit bhi hona padataa he

 Fazle Gufran, who has been doing journalism for more than a decade in the film world, has written the book 'main Hain Villain' on the journey of Bollywood villains, in which he has expressed about the ups and downs in the life and career of more than 101 villains
 
 fajaale gupran ne 40-50 saal peeche jaakar un khalnaayakon ko dhund kar apane kitaab main jivit kar diya, jinhen aaj ke daur main log bhul chuke hai
